< Review>
Besides the fact that Enterprise is extremely overpriced, the staff is super nice, willing to do anything to make you satisfied. I've actually never seen such a professional and helpful attitude before.
In my experience, I did an online reservation. When I picked the car up, the gas tank was nearly empty, and the windscreen washer fluid wasn't replenished. Also at the dealership, I found out that the already high price didn't even include the additional insurance coverage. After adding that, it made the cost 2 times higher than the price of their competition (Avis, hertz,...).
The car was quite new (just 7 000 miles) and more or less clean.
Afterwards, I returned the car with nearly a full tank of gas (instead of the original empty tank) as I had to cancel a part of my trip and didn't use all the gas as I planed.
They asked if I was satisfied, they took my criticism and offered to give me a discount and refund me for the extra fuel. I came there angry and was leaving in a positive mood. It was a very pro-customer oriented attitude. I guess the extra high cost is paid for the customer oriented approach. If it's worth the high price, that's what everyone has to figure out for themselves.< /Review>

< review>
I will start off by saying that all of the gentlemen that work at this location are extremely friendly and helpful, so no complaints there. My complaint has to do with the car that I rented which I ended up having to exchange. I rented an SUV and was originally given a black Nissan Rouge. Had I smelled how strong the vehicle had smelled of weed and cigarettes, I would have requested a vehicle change immediately. However, I had a mask on and couldn't smell anything.

We had intended on leaving for our vacation later that night but after smelling how terrible the car smelled we couldn't leave because the smell was absolutely unbearable. I have 2 kids and one being an infant. I couldn't subject my children to the terrible smell it was almost sickening. Not to mention there was some sort of device on the passenger side of the front window. It's not legal in California to have anything on your windshield that may obstruct your view. I was worried I would be pulled over because of it. Could you imagine a African American being pulled over with a car reeking of weed with 2 kids in the car? Ya...not cool.

Long story short, we couldn't leave the day we had intended on leaving because of the above. I called  early the next day and requested a vehicle change. I was offered 10% which was nice but considering the situation I should have had the first day free.<//review>

<date>1578197371605</date>< Rating>

< Review>
I want to start off by mentioning I have never provided a review on an establishment before; however, after my experience at Blue Granite today, I felt compelled to do so.

My two sons ages 8 and 12 have shown a recent interest in learning to climb. I took them to Blue Granite on a Saturday at around 10am and was immediately greeted by a very professional young man (Ivan) at the front desk.

Ivan welcomed my family and I and squared my boys away with some climbing shoes and harnesses. We were provided a tour of the beautiful facility and given a very thorough introduction to safety and climbing.

It was not long and my boys were literally climbing all over the walls in the gym.

The facility was exceptionally clean and the other patrons were friendly and helpful to my boys.

Our day pass afforded us the opportunity to leave for a few hours and return at our leisure. We left for lunch and visited family in West Shore then returned the same evening for more climbing as the boys couldn't get enough!

We live in Pollock Pines and will definitely be back to attend more classes to better our knowledge in safe climbing practices with hopes to take this outdoors during the spring and summer months.

Thank you to Ivan and the Blue Granite team for such a memorable experience.< /Review>

<name>Shawn Posey</name><date>1567194794555<//date><review>I reserve this rating for the very few...  this place is LEGIT!
Stopped by on the first visit, grabbed a burrito and from the first bite I knew this place was special.  The meat has excellent seasoning, fresh fixings on the inside served with pride by a staff of family.
It is one of those meals you just keep thinking about, long after mealtime.  It is that good.

Second visit (only a few days later) tried the tacos de adobada.  BOOM! The fresh pressed tortilla complemented the marinated meat, with a little guacamole salsa and salsa verde (they bring you an array of choices for the sauces)... three wasn't enough (oh, believe me... I WAS FULL)... I ordered two more... this wasn't because the portions were small... I just wasn't ready to quit eating yet.

Stupid 3-day weekend... I eat here during work, now I'm three days away from trying the next menu item.

If you are traveling on the freeway, this is literally two blocks off the exit (just over the railroad tracks-easy on and off with VERY quick service); it will NOT disappoint.<//review>< Pictures>

< Text>
This must rank as one of the greatest experiences of my life.  The sky was blue, the water sapphire, the balloon red and yellow-perfect colors.  We could see how difficult it is to launch a balloon and how the crew worked collaboratively to make the experience happen.  But the liftoff from and the landing  on the boat made the experience unique.  Captain Sheldon took pictures of us, explained the history of ballooning, played music to fit the motion, and made us all laugh.  At the same time, we felt complete trust in his skills.  All the time he was in direct contact with the boat.  As they all said, "Safety first."  The ride is not cheap, but you will not regret spending the money on a once in a lifetime experience.</Text>

< review>
This was one of the most epic experiences I've ever had.  When you get there you will immediately realize that you are in great hands with the staff.  George greeted us warmly, and with a quick signature we were off to the boat.  The staff goes out of there way to make you feel safe and it was comforting to be informed of their precautionary measures.  The whole staff introduced themselves, and Greg, the Captain of the boat stood out as being really friendly and knowledgeable about the area and balloon.  The boat ride itself is beautiful and exciting (knowing you are about to be up in the sky).  The main event was unlike anything I'd done before, watching the balloon inflate just added to the anticipation.  The pilots name was Sheldon, and he was amazing.... his enthusiasm rubbed off on everyone, and you could tell he was incredibly skilled with the balloon.  The tricks he pulled off with the balloon were incredible.  He touched down into the water twice, got up to 2500 ft above the lake, and literally grazed the trees! It was absolutely amazing and I want to go up again!  If you've never been in a hot air balloon, or even if you have, call up Lake Tahoe Balloons and try this incredible experience out!  Shout out to Greg, Sheldon, Blake, George, and the rest of the staff!

-Hotdad<//review>

< Review>
This was our 20th anniversary. It was wonderful. I thought I would be scared because of the heights, however it was wonderful. It goes up subtly and gradually. You don't even know you're moving even going in the middle of the lake. Looking back toward the shoreline is absolutely breathtaking. The winds were calm. The water was calm.  It was just so serene and peaceful. Breathing the clean air was absolutely refreshing. I would suggest this for anybody who wanted to do it. The only thing I would suggest depending on where you're from would dictate how you are dressed. We are from the Seattle area and we did not need to dress as heavy as we thought we needed to be. Yes it is hot in the basket so wearing a hoodie with a couple layers of clothes is way out of the question. The morning was beautiful but as the day progressed it did get very warm. We were back by 11am. So dress accordingly to how you normally would. Everybody was wonderful. Can't say enough about the crew. They're just wonderful made everybody feel at home. It was like a bunch of friends going out on the lake.< /Review>

{'time': 1499731029019, 'text': "Dear Reviewer,\nThank you so much for taking the time to review your phone experience with our office staff. We very much pride ourselves in our customer service and your feedback is valuable. I sincerely hope that your call was somehow disconnected or dropped rather than one of our office staff hanging up on you, however, if they did hand up on you, I'm so very sorry. I have spoken to all of our phone staff and shared your concerns with them. They are all aware at how disappointed and dismayed I was to read about the experience you described in your review. Our pilots, captains and crew are so dedicated to providing you a wonderful experience that it's heart breaking to see the office dropped the ball. I sincerely hope you give us all a second shot.\n\nTo answer your question about why we were closed when you called, we are weather dependent so our season runs mid-May through October. The lake elevation of Lake Tahoe is over 6200 feet and because of that, we can get some pretty extreme winter weather. With temperatures often dropping below freezing at night and remaining below freezing for extended periods of time during the winter months, the marina where our boat is docked often freezes solid. This makes it impossible to get out of the marina to the lake. In addition, our winter storms often bring strong winds. Strong winds are not favorable to balloon flights over Lake Tahoe. Thus we wait until the weather improves in May before we start flying.\n\nAgain, I appreciate your feedback and am very very sorry for your experience on the phone. I do encourage you to give us another chance because between our fantastic Tahoe team and the spectacular Lake Tahoe views, I truly believe you will have a wonderful time.\n\nSincerely\nGabriel Gundling\nOwner"}</resp>

<rate>4< /rate>< review>
So glad I found this place to fulfill my chicken teriyaki craving near work!

I used to go to Flame Broiler a lot but I wanted to try a different place for lunch. I ordered their Spicy Chicken Bowl with brown rice and it was delicious! The meat was cooked very well and I like the slight spicy kick you get from the sauce. You also get the option to add on green onions, if you want. The service was great and it was reasonably priced. And they give you generous portions!

The only downside is that the parking lot is really small so you may have to find parking on the street.< /review>
